margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. &#9744;</p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:4.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #7f7f7f">&#160;</p></div></div> <p style="page-break-before:always"></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"> <p style="margin-top:0pt; A copy of this press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated in this Item 2.02 by reference.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item 2.02, including the exhibit attached hereto, and the information under Item 7.01 below, shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section.  </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Reports Fiscal 2023 First Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">Results On Track to Achieve Full-Year Adjusted EPS Guidance; Company Raises Sales Guidance </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>First quarter financial highlights </I></P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting a $6.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge recognized in connection with the previously announced opioid litigation settlement frameworks and certain other
opioid-related matters </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

growth of 53.1&nbsp;percent in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting higher <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccine volumes </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> cash proceeds of $3&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Fiscal 2023 outlook and long-term growth outlook<SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> </I></P>

fiscal year 2022 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> execution, and currency headwinds </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Raising full-year sales guidance to $133.5&nbsp;billion to $137.5&nbsp;billion reflecting Summit Health acquisition,
refreshed currency rates, and first quarter sales ahead of expectations </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">U.S. Healthcare targets raised with Summit Health announcement on November&nbsp;7, 2022, including fiscal year 2025 sales
goal to $14.5&nbsp;billion to $16.0&nbsp;billion, up from $11.0&nbsp;billion to $12.0&nbsp;billion previously, and positive adjusted EBITDA expected for the segment by the end of fiscal year 2023 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="6%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Increased clarity into the Company&#146;s long-term growth algorithm, building to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-teens</FONT> adjusted EPS growth in fiscal year 2025 and beyond </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#151; January&nbsp;5, 2023
&#151; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2023, which ended November&nbsp;30, 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Chief Executive Officer Rosalind Brewer said: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;WBA delivered a solid start to
the fiscal year, as we continue to accelerate our transformation to a consumer-centric healthcare company. We&#146;re making significant progress in driving our U.S. Healthcare segment to scale and profit, including the recent VillageMD acquisition
of Summit Health. Our core retail pharmacy businesses in both the United States and United Kingdom remain resilient in challenging operating environments. Execution across segments reinforces our confidence in achieving full-year guidance, and our
strategic actions are creating long-term shareholder value.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a
forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort and the Company is unable to address the probable
significance of the unavailable information. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP
measure </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">1 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Overview of First Quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA first quarter sales decreased 1.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $33.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of
1.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Excluding the negative impact from AllianceRx Walgreens of 485 basis points and the positive contributions from U.S. Healthcare M&amp;A of 280 basis points, sales growth was 3.2&nbsp;percent on a
constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss was $6.2&nbsp;billion in the first quarter compared to operating income of $1.3&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Operating loss in the quarter reflects a $6.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation. Adjusted operating income was
$1.0&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 42.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower volumes of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing compared to the peak prior year period, planned payroll and IT
investments in U.S. Retail Pharmacy and growth investments in U.S. Healthcare. This was partly offset by improved retail contributions in the U.S. and International. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net loss in the first quarter was $3.7&nbsp;billion compared to net income of $3.6&nbsp;billion in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. This
decrease is driven by a $5.2&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation offset by a $0.9&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain from the partial sale of
the Company&#146;s equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen during the first quarter; and lapping $2.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> gain on the Company&#146;s investments in VillageMD and Shields Health
Solutions in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted net earnings was $1.0&nbsp;billion, down 30.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, primarily driven by lower adjusted operating income partly offset by the
favorable impact of a lower tax rate compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter primarily due to the release of valuation allowance related to capital loss carryforwards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Loss per share in the first quarter was $4.31, compared to earnings per share of $4.13 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted
earnings per share decreased 30.8&nbsp;percent to $1.16, reflecting a decrease of 29.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net cash provided by operating
activities was $493&nbsp;million in the first quarter. Operating cash flow was negatively impacted by increased inventory build for the U.S. and UK holiday season. Free cash flow was negative $117&nbsp;million, a $762&nbsp;million decrease compared
with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter primarily driven by lower earnings versus the prior year quarter, phasing of working capital, and increased capital expenditures in growth initiatives, including the VillageMD
footprint expansion, the rollout of micro-fulfillment centers, and digital transformation initiatives. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA continues to achieve strong results across its business and strategic priorities, including: </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Build a high-performance culture and a winning team </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="11%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">Eliminated all task-based metrics for retail pharmacy staff, further enabling pharmacists to practice at the top of their
license while creating a differentiated work environment </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Business Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>U.S. Retail Pharmacy: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment had first quarter
sales of $27.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 3.0&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable sales increased 3.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter while
lapping strong comparable sales of 7.9&nbsp;percent in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter included a significant contribution from
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pharmacy sales decreased 4.2&nbsp;percent compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, negatively impacted by a 7.8 percentage point headwind from AllianceRx Walgreens. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 4.8&nbsp;percent in the quarter compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, benefiting from higher branded drug inflation. Comparable prescriptions filled in the first quarter were flat to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, while comparable
prescriptions excluding immunizations increased 2.1&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, a sequential improvement of 220 basis points compared to the prior quarter. Total prescriptions filled in
the quarter, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents, decreased 0.7&nbsp;percent to 311.6&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Retail sales increased 0.8&nbsp;percent and comparable retail sales increased 1.4&nbsp;percent in the first quarter compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Excluding tobacco, comparable retail sales increased 2.1&nbsp;percent, aided by strong cough, cold, flu sales representing a tailwind of 220 bps, partly offset by lower sales of OTC test kits
representing a headwind of 170 basis points. Beauty and personal care categories both grew, benefiting from owned brand offerings and improved inventory availability. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 7.3&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted gross profit decreased 7.2&nbsp;percent.
Gross profit and adjusted gross profit were driven by lower contributions from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations and testing and reimbursement net of procurement savings, partially offset by higher retail gross profit
from higher sales and gross margin expansion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Selling, general and administrative expenses (SG&amp;A) increased 129.8&nbsp;percent from $5.1&nbsp;billion in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $11.7&nbsp;billion. SG&amp;A in the quarter reflects a $6.5&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> charge for opioid-related claims and litigation. Adjusted SG&amp;A
increased 2.5&nbsp;percent to $4.9&nbsp;billion, driven by $100&nbsp;million of increased labor investments, and incremental IT and digital investments, partly offset by cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss in the first quarter was $5.8&nbsp;billion compared to operating income of $1.4&nbsp;billion from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, reflecting the $6.5&nbsp;billion charge for opioid-related claims and litigation. Adjusted operating income decreased 34.6&nbsp;percent to $1.1&nbsp;billion from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting lower
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccination volumes, continued reimbursement pressure, and planned labor investments, partly offset by improved higher retail gross profit from higher sales and gross margin expansion. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">3 </FONT></P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>International: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The
International segment had first quarter sales of $5.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 10.8&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, held back by an adverse currency impact of 15.4&nbsp;percent. Sales increased
4.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, with Boots UK sales growing 4.3&nbsp;percent, and the Company&#146;s Germany wholesale business growing 4.2&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales decreased 0.9&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, due to lower demand for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> services compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots UK comparable retail sales increased 8.7&nbsp;percent compared to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, growing market share for the 7th consecutive quarter. Footfall improved by around 8&nbsp;percent, compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Boots.com continued
to perform well, accounting for 18&nbsp;percent of retail sales in the quarter compared to 9&nbsp;percent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic.</FONT> In November, Boots.com percent of sales reached almost 23&nbsp;percent, including the
biggest ever single day of digital sales for the business, on Black Friday. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit decreased 13.0&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including an adverse currency impact of 15.1&nbsp;percent. Gross profit increased 2.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting higher UK retail sales growth, and strong execution in
our Germany wholesale business, partially offset by lower demand for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related services in the UK and the adverse gross margin impact of National Health Service pharmacy funding. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">SG&amp;A in the quarter decreased 18.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $944&nbsp;million, reflecting a favorable
currency impact of 14.9&nbsp;percent, lower acquisition-related costs, and lower costs related to the Transformational Cost Management Program compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased
5.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting increased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-store</FONT> and marketing activities, higher inflation, and the expiration of temporary <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related
rental reductions received in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating income increased 96.5&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to $106&nbsp;million, reflecting lower acquisition related costs and restructuring activity, partially offset by an adverse currency impact of 18.8&nbsp;percent. Adjusted operating income decreased
28.9&nbsp;percent to $116&nbsp;million, a decrease of 20.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, as strong growth in UK retail and Germany was more than offset by lower
demand for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related services in the UK, the adverse gross margin impact of NHS pharmacy funding, and the expiration of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> rental reductions received in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>U.S. Healthcare: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The U.S. Healthcare segment had first quarter sales of $989&nbsp;million, an increase of $938&nbsp;million compared to the prior year period. On a pro forma basis, this
segment&#146;s businesses grew sales at a combined rate of 38.4&nbsp;percent in the quarter. VillageMD grew 48.7&nbsp;percent, reflecting existing clinic growth and clinic footprint expansion. Shields grew 44.1&nbsp;percent, driven by recent
contract wins, further expansion of existing partnerships, and strong executional focus. CareCentrix grew 22.3&nbsp;percent as a result of additional service offerings with existing partners. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Gross profit was $17&nbsp;million and adjusted gross profit was $43&nbsp;million. Shields and CareCentrix gross profit was more than offset by the VillageMD expansion.
VillageMD added 119 clinics compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter for a total of 375 total clinics open. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">First quarter SG&amp;A
was $454&nbsp;million, and adjusted SG&amp;A was $195&nbsp;million. Adjusted SG&amp;A increased $162&nbsp;million compared to the prior year quarter, due to the year-over-year impact of acquisitions and higher investments in the organic business.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Operating loss was $436&nbsp;million. Adjusted operating loss was $152&nbsp;million, which excludes certain costs related to stock compensation expense and
amortization of acquired intangible assets. Adjusted EBITDA was negative $124&nbsp;million, reflecting a full quarter of VillageMD results compared to six days of results in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter and growth in
organic business investments, partly offset by positive contributions from Shields and CareCentrix. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">4 </FONT></P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA will
hold a conference call to discuss the first quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, January&nbsp;5, 2023. A live simulcast as well as related presentation materials will be available through WBA&#146;s investor relations website
at: https://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com. A replay of the conference will be archived on the website for at least 12 months after the event. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">*All references
to net earnings or net loss are to net earnings or net loss attributable to WBA, and all references to EPS are to diluted EPS attributable to WBA. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">**&#147;Adjusted,&#148; &#147;constant currency&#148; and free cash flow amounts are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. See the
appendix to this release for a discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, including a reconciliation to the most closely correlated GAAP measure. The Company defines Adjusted EBITDA as segment operating
income/(loss) before depreciation, amortization, and stock-based compensation; in addition to these items, the Company excludes certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments, when they occur, as further defined. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:13pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:13pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an
integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">170-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 13,000 locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the
healthcare ecosystem. The Company is reimagining local healthcare and well-being for all as part of its purpose &#150; to create more joyful lives through better health. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to a wide range of health
services, providing high quality health and beauty products and offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">WBA employs more than 325,000 people and has a presence in nine countries through its portfolio of consumer brands: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty
Company, Benavides in Mexico and Ahumada in Chile. Additionally, WBA has a portfolio of healthcare-focused investments located in several countries, including China and the U.S. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA has been recognized for
its commitment to operating sustainably: the Company is an index component of the Dow Jones Sustainability Indices (DJSI) and was named to the 100 Best Corporate Citizens 2022. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">More Company information is available at www.walgreensbootsalliance.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:80pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(WBA-ER)</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The following information
provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented
in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The Company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not calculated or presented in
accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">These
supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the Company&#146;s financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency
translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
Company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the Company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute
for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company does not provide
a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis where it is unable to provide a meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available
without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet occurred, are out of the Company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact
diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Constant currency </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company also presents certain information related to
current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange
rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The Company presents such constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the U.S. reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this
presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Comparable sales
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least
twelve consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster, in the past twelve months as well as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable sales for the
first twelve months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first twelve months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable
retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the Company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same
as other retailers&#146; methods. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail sales, are presented
on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">10 </FONT></P>


</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company considers certain metrics, such as comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions, comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, number of payor/ provider partnerships, number of locations of Walgreens Health Corners, number of VillageMD <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-located</FONT> clinics and number of
total VillageMD clinics, at period end, to be key performance indicators because the Company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the Company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a
substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">With respect to the total number of VillageMD clinics, clinics are defined as the primary care locations where the Company or the Company&#146;s affiliates lease or
license space and the providers are employed by either the Company or one of the Company&#146;s affiliates. These clinics are primarily branded as Village Medical where the Company employs the providers but, in some instances, may operate under
their own brands. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain legal
proceedings, including legal defense costs. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of
the Company&#146;s operating performance. These charges are recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. During the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2022, the Company recorded a $6.5&nbsp;billion charge related to the previously
announced opioid litigation settlement frameworks and certain other opioid-related matters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program charges are costs associated with a formal restructuring plan. These charges are
primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and
contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated
by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an
intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to
measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments exclude the expected profit margin
component from cost of sales recorded under the business combination accounting principles. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting
and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these
arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include charges incurred related to certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in operating income, for example, costs related to integration efforts for merger, acquisition
and divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance and stock compensation. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing
and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the U.S. Retail Pharmacy segment inventory is accounted for
using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices,
which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in foreign
subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within Other income, net. We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying derivative
instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">8</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on business combinations due to the remeasurement of previously held minority equity interests
and debt securities to fair value. During the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2021, the Company recorded such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gains of $2.2&nbsp;billion and $402&nbsp;million for VillageMD and Shields,
respectively. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">9</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gains on the sale of equity method investments. During the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2022,
the Company recorded a gain of $969&nbsp;million in Other income, net due to a partial sale of its equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">10</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax (benefit) provision include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax (benefit) provision commensurate
with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. and UK tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income
tax (benefit) provision. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">11</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax earnings (loss) from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share of certain
equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are recorded within
post tax earnings (loss) from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating to equity
method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations in that
they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">12</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from the reported net loss, the impact of potentially dilutive securities on the
per share amounts has been omitted from the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted EPS for the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

for adjusted diluted net earnings per common share calculation purposes for the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2022. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">The Company reconciles Adjusted EBITDA for U.S. Healthcare segment to Operating loss as the closest GAAP measure for the
segment profitability. The Company does not measure Net earnings attributable to Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. for its segments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets, inventory valuation
adjustments and stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangible assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks, developed technology and
contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements. The revenue generated
by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an
intangible asset becomes impaired, or the estimated useful life of an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to
measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments exclude the expected profit margin
component from cost of sales recorded under the business combination accounting principles. The stock-based compensation fair valuation adjustment reflects the difference between the fair value based remeasurement of awards under purchase accounting
and the grant date fair valuation. Post-acquisition compensation expense recognized in excess of the original grant date fair value of acquiree awards are excluded from the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as these
arise from acquisition-related accounting requirements or agreements, and are not reflective of normal operating activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include charges incurred related to certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities recorded in operating income, for example, costs related to integration efforts for merger, acquisition
and divestitures activities. Examples of such costs include deal costs, severance and stock compensation. These charges are primarily recorded within Selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing
and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Includes U.S. GAAP stock-based compensation expense excluding expenses related to acquisition-related amortization and
acquisition-related costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#acacac">16 </FONT></P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property, plant and
equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other contractual
obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
